12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: Definition - Statistics statistics as a scientific method of collection of theories and techniques of summarising numerical information to make sense out of it. Numerical information or data are numbers with a context as statistics in brief, is the science of data and the art of examining them.Studying statistics can help us feel much comfortable while handling and interpreting a set of figures and numbers.Engineers often study data on quality and reliability of the manufactured products.
12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: Data is defined as known or assumed facts and figures from which conclusion can be drawn. Data are used to make decisions
12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: to support decisions already made, to provide reasons behind happening of certain events and to make predictions of events to come. Some kind of analysis is required to convert data into information.
12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: Statistics means 'numerical description' of facts and in common usage. The term statistics has dual meaning. Statistics in plural sense means data, i.e. the numerical information arising out of the events in connection with any sphere of human experience when a host of uncontrolled causes are acting together. On the other hand, statistics in singular sense, refers to the field or discipline of study. It deals with a methods of analysis of data. In this sense, statistics is defined as the scientific methods required for collections classifying, summarising, analysing and interpreting numerical information.
12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: Recently, a new definition of statistics has evolved. This definition defines statistics not as a body of methods, nor as a collection of data.
12/14/21, 11:44 - +91 86708 58610: , but has an activity. It says that statistics is to increase our understanding to promote human welfare and to improve our quality of life and well-being by advancing the discovery and effective use of knowledge from data. The data with all their uncertainty, variability.

12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: Regarding the methodology used in analysis of data two broad mass of statistics can be identified. Those two branches of statistics are are descriptive statistics and inferential statistics.
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: Descriptive statistics provides the numerical and graphical method to look for the patterns in the dataset. It deals with the collection, organisation, summarisation.
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: and presentation of data in a convenient form.
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: Inferential statistics discusses the ways of making prediction or drawing conclusion about population characteristics based on the data collected.
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: Scope of statistics : In India, study of statistics as a scientific discipline and it's application was introduced by Prof. Prashanta Chandra Mohalanovis in early 1920s.
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: He came in contact with two outstanding statistician - Karl Pearson and R. A. Fizher. He Become interested their work and implied to do research on the works. He formed a group of scientists to work together on the development of stats.later In 1931 he founded Indian Statistical Institute for the study and research in statistics, initially housed at Physics Department, Presidency College, Kolkata.In 1951 it was shifted to its present place(BT Road, Dakshineswar, Kolkata).
12/15/21, 11:28 - +91 86708 58610: Misuses of Statistics:There are some sayings like: "There are three kind of Lies -Lies, Damn Lies and Statistics""An ounce of truth will produce tons of Statistics. "Real figures and numbers cannot lie. Wrong Pictures may come out due to fallible data or interpretation. Statistics is rather useful in extracting and establishing the truth behind the data but it must be used in proper perspective.

12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: Classification of collection of data Any set of data contains some information about certain group of individuals. Thse individuals are called units. The entire group of individuals that we want info about is called population. A part of the population which we actually study in order to gather information is called sample.The complete list of individuals or units in the population is called sampling frame. The sampling frame is very essential for the purpose of drawing the sample from the population. While studying a population we focus on one or more characteristics of the units in the
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: population. For e.g., we may be interested in characteristics, like age, gender blood group
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: , monthly phone bills etc.These are known as variable(s).
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: The name "variable" is derived from the fact "that the characteristics under study".
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: ..study may vary from individual to another."
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: Measurement is the process of assigning values to the variables.
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: These values corresponding to an individuals are called observations
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: A single data value is obtained when a variable is actually measured on an unit. A collection of measurements or observations on one or more variables is called a dataset.
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: A data consisting observations on single variable is known as a "univariant data set"
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: and two (or more) variables is known as "bivariate" or "multivariate".
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: "univariate", not "univariant" (sorry)
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: When data are collected, the observations obtained from each unit of a population or a sample are recorded in the sequence they become available. The sequence of data before they are processed are called "raw data". When data are collected for every unit of a population it is called "census or complete enumeration", sampling otherwise.
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: Clasification of data depends on the type of variable we measure.We can observe different types of variables in practice each of which belongs to any category of the following broad classification - Variable - qualitative / categorical -quantitative / numerical
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: Qualitative -| - ordinal| - non-ordinal Quantitative -| - Discrete| - Continuous . The variable which cannot be measured nuerically but can be measured by their quality is called "qualitative variable". Since these variables place individuals in different categories they are also called "categorical variables or attributes"
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: There are some categorical variables where the categories can be arranged in natural order, i.e. from Small to Big or from High to Low etc. Those variables are called "Ordinal Categorical" variables. For e.g. Income Group may be classified as High, Medium and Low etc.
12/20/21, 11:35 - +91 86708 58610: In Other type of categorical variable , no idea of order among the categories exists. They are called "Non-Ordinal". For e.g. Blood Group, Religion, Marital Status etc. A variable which can be measured numerically is called "Quantitative / Numerical" variable. E.g. - Height, Weight, House Rent etc.

12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: Statistics
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: Data where the values of the variable occur repeatedly and are expressed as the statement of possible variate values together with respective frequencies the number of times of occurence of that particular value in the dataset are called frequency data
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: Data arranged or recorded in the form of series are called non-frequency data / series data. Non-frequency data are of two types - 1) Time Series data, and 2) Cross sectional data.
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: The data collected on the same unit for the same variable for different points or periods of time are called "Time Series data"Average Prices of houses of Calcutta for the years 1990 - 2002, Export of tea in last 12 months are the examples of Time Series data.
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: Such data arise due to the change in variable values over time
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: The data collected on different units for the same point or periods of time are called "Cross Sectional data". The present prices of same cars of different make is an example of Cross Sectional data. In particular, if cross sectional data relate to different  places, then it is called Spital (or Geographical) Series data, such as maximum temperature of different cities in India on a particular day, total population of different states as per 2011 census.
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: The data that are measured across two dimensions, time and cross section are called Panel data. For example, the data on petroleum prices for last seven years in five cities  in India
12/22/21, 11:34 - +91 86708 58610: -- Collection Of Data --Every statistical investigation begins with a definite objective and collection of data is the first step towards achieving this objective. At the time of collecting data, we have to keep the following basic points in mind what purpose the data are expected to serve, what the related variables are and what the target population, i.e. what individuals the data are going to describe. There are two sources of data, 1) Primary source and 2) Secondary source. Primary source is a source where data collected directly from the field of enqquiry and Secondary source where data originally collected by someone are available in a published form.

1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: ----------Stats 25th Jan-------
1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: ```Relative Frequency```
1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: Relative Frequency of a variate value (or class of values) is the proportion of observations corresponding to that particular value (or class). It is obtained by dividing the respective frequency by the total frequency and is given by:Relative frequency of a variate value = Frequency of that value / total frequencyIt lies between 0 and 1. The relative frequencies of all values in a dataset adds upto 1. It gives the relative importance of a variate value in relation to the total frequency and thus makes two or more similar types of datasets comparable.Sometimes, the relative frequencies are expressed in percentage as (frequency / total frequency * 100), i.e., (relative frequency * 100) which is known as percent frequency. Expressed as percents, the present frequency of all values should add up to 100. Sometimes, this total may deviate little from 100 because of the error due to rounding off the values.
1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: ```Frequency Distribution of a Discrete Variable```
1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: Here we discuss how to construct a frequency distribution of a discrete variable from a raw dataset. In this connection we will also define the cumulative frequency -- Less than type & More than type. We use Tally marks for the purpose of counting the frequencies conveniently, for each value of the variable. First we list all possible values of the variable in ascending order. Then we put a tally against each value of the variable in the dataset. Each tally represents one frequency. We read off each observation in the raw dataset and for each one we put a tally againtst the corresponding variate value in the frequency table and finally we count the tally marks for each variate value. This helps us counting the frequencies for each value of the variable and minimizes the chance of making errors in counting the frequencies from raw data.
1/25/22, 11:29 - +91 86708 58610: We make a group of five tallies (/////) in order to avoid error in counting a large number of tallies.Cumulative Frequency of 'Less than type' corresponding to each variate value is obtained by cumulating or adding frequencies successively from the top of the frequency distribution upto the frequency of that value. i.e. Adding its frequency to the frequency of all the values of the variable smaller than that. Similarly, the cumulative frequency of 'More than type' for each variate value is obtained by adding it's frequency to the frequencies of all variate values higher than that. Thus we can obtain cumulative freuencies of 'Less than type' ('More than type') by adding frequencies successively starting from the top(bottom) of the frequency table.
